    <h2 class="title" style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; color:rgb(112,112,112); font-weight:normal; font-size:2.769em; line-height:1.167; margin-top:0px">
     设备控制台 (DevCon.exe) 示例
    </h2>
    <div id="mainSection" style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; clear:both; color:rgb(42,42,42); font-size:13px; line-height:17.55px">

     <h3 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.692em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_devcon_examples_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_DEVCON_EXAMPLES_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
     </h3>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      本部分提供以下设备控制台 (DevCon.exe) 命令的示例：

       <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">

     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="devcon_dp_add__dp_deleted__dp_enum" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DEVCON_DP_ADD__DP_DELETED__DP_ENUM" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      DevCon dp_add、dp_deleted、dp_enum
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff545861" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       示例 45：添加和删除驱动程序包
      </a>
     </p>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_1_find_all_hardware_ids_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_1_FIND_ALL_HARDWARE_IDS_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 1：查找所有硬件 ID
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      由于 DevCon 操作使用 ID 和 ID 模式来标识设备，因此使用 DevCon 的第一个常用步骤就是为计算机上的设备创建一个硬件 ID 参考文件。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544772" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon HwIDs
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作，该操作返回 ID 以及设备描述。该命令使用通配符 (
      <strong>
       *
      </strong>
      ) 来表示本地计算机上的所有设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-1" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_0688589b-bdae-4186-ac97-a28fc7548bc3" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon hwids *

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      由于输出较长并且重复使用，因此将输出保存在文本文件中以供参考。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用通配符 (
      <strong>
       *
      </strong>
      ) 来表示计算机上的所有设备。该命令使用重定向字符 (
      <strong>
       &gt;
      </strong>
      ) 将该命令输出保存在 hwids.txt 文件中。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-2" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_18acf4fa-b0be-4512-9119-da4825919307" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon hwids * &gt; hwids.txt

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令查找远程计算机 Server01 上设备的硬件 ID。该命令使用
      <strong>
       /m
      </strong>
      参数来指定远程计算机的名称。该命令将输出重定向到 server01_hwids.txt 文件以供日后参考。
     </p>
     <div class="note">
      <strong>
       注意
      </strong>
      除非用户在此远程计算机上具有所需的权限，否则该命令将会失败。若要在远程计算机上运行 DevCon 命令，组策略设置必须允许即插即用服务在远程计算机上运行。在运行 Windows Vista 和 Windows 7 的计算机上，默认情况下组策略将禁止对此服务的远程访问。在运行 Windows 驱动程序工具包 (WDK) 8.1 和 Windows 驱动程序工具包 (WDK) 8 的计算机上，远程访问不可用。
     </div>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-3" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_edee09e0-eb2f-43db-9049-9c570ae31c60" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /m:\\server01 hwids * &gt; server01_hwids.txt

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_2_find_hardware_ids_by_using_a_pattern_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_2_FIND_HARDWARE_IDS_BY_USING_A_PATTERN_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 2：使用模式查找硬件 ID
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      若要查找某个特定设备的硬件 ID，请输入硬件 ID 或模式、兼容的 ID 或模式、设备实例 ID 或模式或者设备安装程序类的名称。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <strong>
       DevCon HwIDs
      </strong>
      操作和模式来查找计算机上软盘驱动器的硬件 ID。（用户假定模式出现在其中一个设备标识符中。）该命令使用通配符 (
      <strong>
       *
      </strong>
      ) 来表示任何 ID 中可能位于单词“floppy”之前或之后的所有字符。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-4" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_736273ac-dd4d-4f6e-bee7-d400d2b73433" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon hwids *floppy*

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示计算机上软盘驱动器的设备实例 ID、硬件 ID 以及兼容的 ID。可以在后续的 DevCon 命令中使用这些 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-5" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_cfec6dde-e4a9-4ccd-b53c-9ca8c8c08336" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">FDC\GENERIC_FLOPPY_DRIVE\5&amp;39194F6D&amp;0&amp;0
    Name: Floppy disk drive
    Hardware ID's:
        FDC\GENERIC_FLOPPY_DRIVE
    Compatible ID's:
        GenFloppyDisk
1 matching device(s) found.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在本例中，短语“floppy”出现在计算机上唯一一个设备的硬件 ID 或兼容的 ID 中。如果它在多个设备的 ID 中出现，那么其 ID 中包含“floppy”的所有设备都会出现在输出中。
     </p>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_3_find_hardware_ids_by_using_a_class_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_3_FIND_HARDWARE_IDS_BY_USING_A_CLASS_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 3：使用类查找硬件 ID
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544772" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon HwIDs
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作和设备安装程序类来查找“端口”设备安装程序类中所有设备的硬件 ID。类名称前面的等号 (
      <strong>
       =
      </strong>
      ) 表示它是一个类，而不是 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-6" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_2d37832d-4d1b-4806-a37c-d9ee8e6cb0a9" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon hwids =ports

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示端口安装程序类中三个设备的硬件 ID 以及兼容的 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-7" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_93bd86fb-c822-4cca-9894-11dd24046c8c" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ACPI\PNP0401\4&amp;B4063F4&amp;0
    Name: ECP Printer Port (LPT1)
    Hardware ID's:
        ACPI\PNP0401
        *PNP0401
ACPI\PNP0501\1
    Name: Communications Port (COM1)
    Hardware ID's:
        ACPI\PNP0501
        *PNP0501
ACPI\PNP0501\2
    Name: Communications Port (COM2)
    Hardware ID's:
        ACPI\PNP0501
        *PNP0501
3 matching device(s) found.

        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_4_list_classes_on_the_local_computer_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_4_LIST_CLASSES_ON_THE_LOCAL_COMPUTER_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 4：列出本地计算机上的类
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      由于 DevCon 操作可以使用设备安装程序类来标识设备，因此它对于创建计算机上设备的设备安装程序类的参考文件非常有用。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544712" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Classes
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作，该操作返回计算机上所有类的列表和描述。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-8" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_80f3da2a-f7fa-4389-9524-a8eeae6f4ac6" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon classes

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      由于输出较长并且重复使用，因此将输出保存在文本文件中以供参考。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令显示计算机上的所有设备类。该命令使用重定向字符 (
      <strong>
       &gt;
      </strong>
      ) 将该命令输出保存在 classes.txt 文件中。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-9" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">

        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_f6cbd054-5e07-48d0-abc9-9b832d51d237" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon classes &gt; classes.txt

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_5_list_classes_on_the_remote_computer_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_5_LIST_CLASSES_ON_THE_REMOTE_COMPUTER_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 5：列出远程计算机上的类
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544712" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Classes
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作列出远程计算机 Server01 上的设备安装程序类：
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-10" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">

         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /m:\\server01 classes

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      由于输出较长并且重复使用，因此将输出保存在文本文件中以供参考。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用重定向字符 (
      <strong>
       &gt;
      </strong>
      ) 将该命令输出保存在 server01_classes.txt 文件中。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-11" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">

         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /m:\\server01 classes &gt; server01_classes.txt

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>

     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_6_list_the_devices_in_a_device_setup_class_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_6_LIST_THE_DEVICES_IN_A_DEVICE_SETUP_CLASS_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 6：列出设备安装程序类中的设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544785" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon ListClass
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作列出 Net 中的设备、网络适配器的设备安装程序类。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-12" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_007ca810-949b-40ff-8f33-681ab2706b5b" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon listclass net

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 Net 安装程序类中每个设备的设备实例 ID 和描述。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-13" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_6db37ce5-3511-428f-9d52-12e6121dd738" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">Listing 6 device(s) for setup class "Net" (Network adapters).
PCI\VEN_10B7&amp;DEV_9200&amp;SUBSYS_00BE1028&amp;REV_78\4&amp;BB7B4AE&amp;0&amp;60F0: 3Com 3C920 Integrated Fast Ethernet Controller (3C905C-TX Compatible)
ROOT\MS_L2TPMINIPORT\0000                                   : WAN Miniport (L2TP)
ROOT\MS_NDISWANIP\0000                                      : WAN Miniport (IP)
ROOT\MS_PPPOEMINIPORT\0000                                  : WAN Miniport (PPPOE)
ROOT\MS_PPTPMINIPORT\0000                                   : WAN Miniport (PPTP)
ROOT\MS_PTIMINIPORT\0000                                    : Direct Parallel

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      此显示尽管非常有趣，但不提供 Net 安装程序类中设备的硬件 ID。以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544772" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon HwIDs
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作列出 Net 安装程序类中的设备。在
      <strong>
       DevCon HwIDs
      </strong>
      命令中，类名称前面有一个等号 (
      <strong>
       =
      </strong>
      ) 用于表示它是一个类，不是 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-14" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_a59d7854-60ed-4d96-976f-4b4cd20d8a8c" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon hwids =net

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      所得到的显示列出 Net 类中的设备并且包含该类中设备的设备实例 ID、硬件 ID 以及兼容的 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-15" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">

        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>

         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">PCI\VEN_10B7&amp;DEV_9200&amp;SUBSYS_00BE1028&amp;REV_78\4&amp;BB7B4AE&amp;0&amp;60F0

      <a id="ddk_example_7_list_the_devices_in_multiple_classes_on_a_remote_compute" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_7_LIST_THE_DEVICES_IN_MULTIPLE_CLASSES_ON_A_REMOTE_COMPUTE" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 7：列出远程计算机上多个类中的设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544785" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon ListClass
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作列出远程计算机 Server01 上 DiskDrive、CDROM 和 TapeDrive 类中的设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-16" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_dbfd5be1-cb4c-47a4-b7ee-f8c6cbf28e4c" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /m:\\server01 listclass diskdrive cdrom tapedrive

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示此远程计算机上这些类中的设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-17" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>

        </div>
       </div>

     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_8_list_all_driver_files_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_8_LIST_ALL_DRIVER_FILES_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 8：列出所有驱动程序文件
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544734" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon DriverFiles
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作列出系统上的设备使用的驱动程序的文件名。该命令使用通配符 (
      <strong>
       *
      </strong>
      ) 来表示系统上的所有设备。由于输出量大，因此该命令使用重定向字符 (
      <strong>
       &gt;
      </strong>
      ) 将输出重定向到参考文件 driverfiles.txt。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-18" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_a25577de-bb29-4d95-aab7-447657b3fd5c" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon driverfiles * &gt; driverfiles.txt

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_9_list_the_driver_files_of_a_particular_device_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_9_LIST_THE_DRIVER_FILES_OF_A_PARTICULAR_DEVICE_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 9：列出特定设备的驱动程序文件
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544734" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon DriverFiles
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作搜索本地计算机上的鼠标设备使用的设备驱动程序。该命令通过硬件 ID HID\Vid_045e&amp;Pid_0039&amp;Rev_0121 来标识设备。硬件 ID 包含在引号中，因为它包含 &amp; 字符 (
      <strong>
       &amp;
      </strong>
      )。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-19" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_778aab34-1c3d-4786-b98b-e50b47139384" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon driverfiles "HID\Vid_045e&amp;Pid_0039&amp;Rev_0121"

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示支持鼠标设备的两个设备驱动程序。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-20" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_7d2afcff-ca8d-4098-8217-68c3687cb537" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">HID\VID_045E&amp;PID_0039\6&amp;DC36FDE&amp;0&amp;0000
    Name: Microsoft USB IntelliMouse Optical
    Driver installed from c:\windows\inf\msmouse.inf [HID_Mouse_Inst]. 2 file(s)

        C:\WINDOWS\System32\DRIVERS\mouhid.sys
        C:\WINDOWS\System32\DRIVERS\mouclass.sys
1 matching device(s) found.

        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_10_list_driver_packages_by_hardware_id_pattern_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_10_LIST_DRIVER_PACKAGES_BY_HARDWARE_ID_PATTERN_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 10：通过硬件 ID 模式列出驱动程序包
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544737" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon DriverNodes
       </strong>
      </a>
      命令和 ID 模式来列出软件枚举的设备的驱动程序节点。模式对于查找可能不在同一安装程序类中的类似设备的信息非常有用。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用 ID 模式
      <strong>
       sw*
      </strong>
      来指定其硬件 ID 或兼容的 ID 以“sw”开头的设备（即，软件枚举的设备）。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-21" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_5edb56f6-736c-439a-93d8-42a9af36741f" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon drivernodes sw*

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示系统上软件枚举的设备的驱动程序节点。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-22" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_137b6b33-d680-4bc8-9d04-b98ae94c375d" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">SW\{A7C7A5B0-5AF3-11D1-9CED-00A024BF0407}\{9B365890-165F-11D0-A195-0020AFD156E4}

        </div>
       </div>

     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_11_list_driver_packages_by_device_instance_id_pattern_tool" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_11_LIST_DRIVER_PACKAGES_BY_DEVICE_INSTANCE_ID_PATTERN_TOOL" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 11：通过设备实例 ID 模式列出驱动程序包
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544737" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon DriverNodes
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作列出其设备实例 ID 以“ROOT\MEDIA”开头的所有设备的驱动程序包（即，位于 Enum\Root\Media 注册表子项中的设备）。该命令使用 at 字符 (
      <strong>
       @
      </strong>
      ) 指示短语位于设备实例 ID 中。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-23" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_f91a3393-03eb-4b86-bfae-907bd446b290" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon drivernodes @ROOT\MEDIA*

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示其设备实例 ID 以“ROOT\MEDIA”开头的驱动程序节点。
     </p>

      <a id="ddk_example_12_list_resources_of_a_class_of_devices_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_12_LIST_RESOURCES_OF_A_CLASS_OF_DEVICES_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 12：列出某个设备类的资源
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544805" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Resources
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作显示分配给 Hdc 设备安装程序类中设备的资源。该类包含 IDE 控制器。“hdc”前面的等号 (
      <strong>
       =
      </strong>
      ) 表示它是一个类，而不是 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-25" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_008c5819-2f51-4522-ae9f-9c026aea78a0" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon resources =hdc

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 列出分配给本地计算机上 IDE 控制器的资源。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-26" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">

      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_13_LIST_RESOURCES_OF_DEVICE_ON_A_REMOTE_COMPUTER_BY_ID_TOO" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">

      示例 13：通过 ID 列出远程计算机上设备的资源
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544805" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Resources
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作列出分配给远程计算机 Server01 上系统计时器的资源。该命令使用系统计时器的硬件 ID ACPI\PNP0100 来指定设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-27" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_df29cb96-49e0-49b7-aabd-97ea96228c49" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /m:\\Server01 resources *PNP0100

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 Server01 系统计时器的资源。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-28" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_b92f603c-e7df-4eef-be3c-effc23368eb9" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ROOT\*PNP0100\PNPBIOS_8
    Name: System timer
    Device has the following resources reserved:
        IO  : 0040-005f
        IRQ : 0

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用 DevCon 资源命令中远程系统计时器的设备实例 ID。at 字符 (
      <strong>
       @
      </strong>
      ) 表示此字符串是一个设备实例 ID，而不是硬件 ID 或兼容的 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-29" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_ae78a747-b3f8-43bb-a766-20c5696623e6" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /m:\\Server01 resources @ACPI\PNP0100\4&amp;b4063f4&amp;0

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>

     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_14_display_the_driver_stack_for_storage_devices_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_14_DISPLAY_THE_DRIVER_STACK_FOR_STORAGE_DEVICES_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 14：显示存储设备的驱动程序堆栈
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544829" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Stack
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作搜索 Volume 安装程序类中的设备并显示这些设备的预期驱动程序堆栈。等号 (
      <strong>
       =
      </strong>
      ) 表示该字符串是类名称。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-30" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_ac29f801-610a-46c4-a0ee-c8aefff60b2d" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon stack =Volume

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 Volume 类中设备的预期堆栈。返回的数据包括每个设备的设备实例 ID 和描述、此设备安装程序类的 GUID 和名称、上一级和下一级筛选器驱动程序以及控制服务（如果有）的名称。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-31" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_5aa98d96-ad4b-4999-8d2e-d9a5144a81da" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">STORAGE\VOLUME\1&amp;30A96598&amp;0&amp;SIGNATURE32323533OFFSET271167600LENGTH6E00D0C00
    Name: Generic volume
    Setup Class: {71A27CDD-812A-11D0-BEC7-08002BE2092F} Volume

        VolSnap
    Controlling service:
        (none)

    Name: Generic volume
    Setup Class: {71A27CDD-812A-11D0-BEC7-08002BE2092F} Volume
    Class upper filters:
        VolSnap
    Controlling service:
        (none)
2 matching device(s) found.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_15_find_the_setup_class_of_a_device_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_15_FIND_THE_SETUP_CLASS_OF_A_DEVICE_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 15：查找设备的安装程序类
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544829" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Stack
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作除了返回上一级和下一级筛选器驱动程序之外，还返回设备的安装程序类。以下命令通过查找其设备实例 ID 查找打印机端口接口的安装程序类，然后使用设备实例 ID 查找其安装程序类。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544772" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon HwIDs
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作通过在打印机端口硬件 ID 中使用短语“LPT”来查找打印机端口接口的设备实例 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-32" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_7d991b65-aeb8-4625-b24a-a940e51c58c3" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon hwids *lpt*

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 返回打印机端口接口的设备实例 ID（以粗体文本显示）以及硬件 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-33" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_87fa2e7c-3134-4424-90d4-da279e39a53a" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">LPTENUM\MICROSOFTRAWPORT\5&amp;CA97D7E&amp;0&amp;LPT1
    Name: Printer Port Logical Interface
    Hardware ID's:
        LPTENUM\MicrosoftRawPort958A
        MicrosoftRawPort958A
1 matching device(s) found.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      下一个命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544829" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Stack
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作查找设备实例 ID 表示的设备的设备安装程序类。at 字符 (
      <strong>
       @
      </strong>
      ) 将此 ID 标识为设备实例 ID。此 ID 包含在引号中，因为它包含 &amp; 字符。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-34" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_2166a08e-a3cd-485f-ae5a-b1400e1403e7" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon stack "@LPTENUM\MICROSOFTRAWPORT\5&amp;CA97D7E&amp;0&amp;LPT1"

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示打印机端口接口的驱动程序堆栈，包括类。显示表明打印机端口位于 System 类中。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-35" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">

        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_3e45869d-663d-451d-982f-37fc6e69b865" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">LPTENUM\MICROSOFTRAWPORT\5&amp;CA97D7E&amp;0&amp;LPT1

      <a id="ddk_example_16_display_the_stack_for_related_devices_on_a_remote_compu" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_16_DISPLAY_THE_STACK_FOR_RELATED_DEVICES_ON_A_REMOTE_COMPU" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 16：显示远程计算机上相关设备的堆栈
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <strong>
       DevCon Stack
      </strong>
      操作显示远程计算机 Server01 上微型端口驱动程序设备的预期堆栈。该命令搜索 Net 安装程序类中其硬件 ID 或兼容的 ID 中包含“miniport”的设备。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      请注意，该命令首先将搜索限制于 Net 安装程序类，然后查找“miniport”字符串。除了 Net 安装程序类中的设备之外，它不会查找其他设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-36" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_f4074afb-1693-4521-b18f-055b68a23a9e" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /m:\\server01 stack =net *miniport*

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 Server01 上微型端口驱动程序的预期堆栈。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-37" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_f6c1878d-c4bd-402c-b6b1-72724297fd81" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ROOT\MS_L2TPMINIPORT\0000
    Name: WAN Miniport (L2TP)

        NdisTapi
ROOT\MS_PPTPMINIPORT\0000

        </div>
       </div>

     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_17_display_the_status_of_all_devices_on_the_local_computer" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_17_DISPLAY_THE_STATUS_OF_ALL_DEVICES_ON_THE_LOCAL_COMPUTER" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 17：显示本地计算机上所有设备的状态
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544831" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Status
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作查找本地计算机上所有设备的状态。然后，将状态保存在 status.txt 文件中以便记录或供日后查看。该命令使用通配符 (
      <strong>
       *
      </strong>
      ) 表示所有设备，使用重定向字符 (
      <strong>
       &gt;
      </strong>
      ) 将输出重定向到 status.txt 文件。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-38" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_8635f7a8-55f8-44b8-b128-78c116cc783a" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon status * &gt; status.txt

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_18_display_the_status_of_a_device_by_device_instance_id_to" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_18_DISPLAY_THE_STATUS_OF_A_DEVICE_BY_DEVICE_INSTANCE_ID_TO" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 18：通过设备实例 ID 显示设备的状态
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      查找特定设备状态的最可靠的方法是使用设备的设备实例 ID。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544831" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Status
       </strong>
      </a>
      命令中本地计算机上 I/O 控制器的设备实例 ID。该命令包含设备的设备实例 ID PCI\VEN_8086&amp;DEV_1130&amp;SUBSYS_00000000&amp;REV_02\3&amp;29E81982&amp;0&amp;00。此 ID 前面的 at 字符 (
      <strong>
       @
      </strong>
      ) 将该字符串标识为设备实例 ID。此 ID 必须包含在引号中，因为它包含 &amp; 字符。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-39" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_f088545b-fac3-4a8c-81dd-037d6f4f6b79" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon status "@PCI\VEN_8086&amp;DEV_1130&amp;SUBSYS_00000000&amp;REV_02\3&amp;29E81982&amp;0&amp;00"

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 I/O 控制器的状态。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-40" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_f6831757-f07e-4e7f-8c44-ceed57c93245" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">PCI\VEN_8086&amp;DEV_1130&amp;SUBSYS_00000000&amp;REV_02\3&amp;29E81982&amp;0&amp;00
    Name: Intel(R) 82815 Processor to I/O Controller - 1130
    Driver is running.
1 matching device(s) found.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_19_display_the_status_of_related_devices_on_a_remote_compu" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_19_DISPLAY_THE_STATUS_OF_RELATED_DEVICES_ON_A_REMOTE_COMPU" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 19：显示远程计算机上相关设备的状态
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544831" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Status
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作显示远程计算机 Server01 上与特定存储有关的设备的状态。该命令搜索以下设备：
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
        磁盘驱动器，GenDisk
       </p>
      </li>
      <li>
       <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
        CD-ROM 驱动器，GenCdRom
       </p>
      </li>
      <li>
       <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
        软盘驱动器，FDC\GENERIC_FLOPPY_DRIVE
       </p>
      </li>
      <li>
       <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
        卷，STORAGE\Volume
       </p>
      </li>
      <li>
       <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
        逻辑磁盘管理器，ROOT\DMIO
       </p>
      </li>
      <li>
       <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
        卷管理器，ROOT\FTDISK
       </p>
      </li>
      <li>
       <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
        软盘控制器，ACPI\PNP0700
       </p>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在该命令中，每个 ID 与其他 ID 之间用空格分隔。请注意，GenDisk 和 GenCdRom 是兼容的 ID，而其他 ID 都是硬件 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-41" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_fca3a0b3-930c-427d-891c-475e68108429" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /m:\\server01 status GenDisk GenCdRom FDC\GENERIC_FLOPPY_DRIVE STORAGE\Volume ROOT\DMIO ROOT\FTDISK ACPI\PNP0700

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示每个设备的状态。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-42" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_e5f0bfd8-e313-47e1-9821-a94c1397cf44" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">FDC\GENERIC_FLOPPY_DRIVE\1&amp;3A2146F1&amp;0&amp;0
    Name: Floppy disk drive
