     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_20_find_devices_by_hardware_id_pattern_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_20_FIND_DEVICES_BY_HARDWARE_ID_PATTERN_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 20：通过硬件 ID 模式查找设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544755" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Find
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作搜索远程计算机 Server01 上的鼠标设备。具体来说，该命令搜索 Server01 计算机中其硬件 ID 或兼容的 ID 包含“mou”的设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-43" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_f0c55c2b-3a5b-400b-bc41-5321301ccc8c" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /m:\\Server01 find *mou*

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在本例中，DevCon 找到两个鼠标设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-44" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_2103196e-2af6-4904-a436-7376e0d91a5e" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ROOT\*PNP0F03\1_0_21_0_31_0                                 : Microsoft PS/2 Mouse
ROOT\RDP_MOU\0000                                           : Terminal Server Mouse Driver

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      由于所有 DevCon 显示操作也查找硬件 ID，因此你可以使用任何显示操作来搜索硬件 ID。根据输出中所需的内容选择操作。例如，若要查找本地计算机上与鼠标相关的设备使用的设备驱动程序，请提交以下命令。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-45" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_1fb9d100-b9c7-4089-8e12-d7965d9a9054" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon driverfiles *mou*

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 查找设备并列出它们的驱动程序。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-46" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_2073f102-d5b2-415e-9c6d-783b26400693" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">HID\VID_045E&amp;PID_0039\6&amp;DC36FDE&amp;0&amp;0000
    Name: Microsoft USB IntelliMouse Optical

     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_21_find_devices_by_device_instance_id_or_class_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_21_FIND_DEVICES_BY_DEVICE_INSTANCE_ID_OR_CLASS_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 21：通过设备实例 ID 或类查找设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544755" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Find
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作显示本地计算机上的所有旧设备。由于旧设备没有硬件 ID，因此你必须通过它们的设备实例 ID（注册表路径）ROOT\LEGACY 或其安装程序类 LegacyDriver 来搜索它们。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      第一个命令通过设备实例 ID 模式查找旧的驱动程序。此 ID 模式前有 at 字符 (
      <strong>
       @
      </strong>
      ) 用于指示设备实例 ID 以及随后的通配符 (
      <strong>
       *
      </strong>
      ) 在 ROOT\Legacy 子项中查找所有设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-47" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_a894226c-6893-4164-b3f8-0d3fa6defbb6" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon find @root\legacy*

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      第二个命令通过搜索 LegacyDriver 类中的所有设备来查找旧的设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-48" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_0f773c3f-8e02-401f-baaa-68632dc4a7df" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon find =legacydriver

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      这两个命令产生相同的输出，在本例中，找到相同的 27 个旧设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-49" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_a8ca373b-9f1a-441d-8731-bf1d3788da29" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ROOT\LEGACY_AFD\0000                                        : AFD Networking Support Environment
ROOT\LEGACY_BEEP\0000                                       : Beep
ROOT\LEGACY_DMBOOT\0000                                     : dmboot
ROOT\LEGACY_DMLOAD\0000                                     : dmload

27 matching device(s) found.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_22_find_and_find_all_devices_in_a_setup_class_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_22_FIND_AND_FIND_ALL_DEVICES_IN_A_SETUP_CLASS_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 22：查找安装程序类中的设备（查找全部）
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544761" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon FindAll
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作查找 Net 安装程序类中的计算机上的所有设备。等号 (
      <strong>
       =
      </strong>
      ) 表示 Net 是安装程序类，而不是 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-50" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_e9e33cc8-19ec-40bb-8db7-1a444defcfc5" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon findall =net

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 列出 Net 安装程序类中的下列 7 个设备。前 6 个是标准的微型端口驱动程序设备。第 7 个设备是 RAS 异步适配器，它是软件枚举的设备 (SW\*)，需要时才会安装。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-51" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_00bb9d9b-7712-4bc3-a753-98b29eb9fb4c" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">PCI\VEN_10B7&amp;DEV_9200&amp;SUBSYS_00BE1028&amp;REV_78\4&amp;BB7B4AE&amp;0&amp;60F0: 3Com 3C920 Integrated Fast
Ethernet Controller (3C905C-TX Compatible)
ROOT\MS_L2TPMINIPORT\0000                                   : WAN Miniport (L2TP)
ROOT\MS_NDISWANIP\0000                                      : WAN Miniport (IP)
ROOT\MS_PPPOEMINIPORT\0000                                  : WAN Miniport (PPPOE)
ROOT\MS_PPTPMINIPORT\0000                                   : WAN Miniport (PPTP)
ROOT\MS_PTIMINIPORT\0000                                    : Direct Parallel
SW\{EEAB7790-C514-11D1-B42B-00805FC1270E}\ASYNCMAC          : RAS Async Adapter
7 matching device(s) found.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令通过运行
      <strong>
       DevCon Find
      </strong>
      命令（使用的参数与之前的
      <strong>
       DevCon FindAll
      </strong>
      命令相同）来比较
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544755" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Find
       </strong>
      </a>
      和
      <strong>
       DevCon FindAll
      </strong>
      操作。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-52" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_e312cb5e-8ae4-4b7d-b987-129be160c1b1" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon find =net

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 列出 Net 安装程序类中的下列 6 个设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-53" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_a03c994a-c1ab-48ac-980f-490e56e0386d" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">PCI\VEN_10B7&amp;DEV_9200&amp;SUBSYS_00BE1028&amp;REV_78\4&amp;BB7B4AE&amp;0&amp;60F0: 3Com 3C920 Integrated Fast
Ethernet Controller (3C905C-TX Compatible)
ROOT\MS_L2TPMINIPORT\0000                                   : WAN Miniport (L2TP)
ROOT\MS_NDISWANIP\0000                                      : WAN Miniport (IP)
ROOT\MS_PPPOEMINIPORT\0000                                  : WAN Miniport (PPPOE)
ROOT\MS_PPTPMINIPORT\0000                                   : WAN Miniport (PPTP)
ROOT\MS_PTIMINIPORT\0000                                    : Direct Parallel
6 matching device(s) found.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      可以预测
      <strong>
       DevCon Find
      </strong>
      命令（仅返回当前安装的设备）不会列出软件枚举的设备，因为该设备未安装。
     </p>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_23_display_the_filter_drivers_for_a_setup_class_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_23_DISPLAY_THE_FILTER_DRIVERS_FOR_A_SETUP_CLASS_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 23：显示某个安装程序类的筛选器驱动程序
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544714" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon ClassFilter
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作显示 DiskDrive 安装程序类中的上一级筛选器驱动程序。由于该命令不包含任何 classfilter 运算符，因此 DevCon 显示该类的筛选器驱动程序，而不更改它们。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-54" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_e80bd9e6-3439-4529-a4ad-b3978510dd2c" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon classfilter DiskDrive upper

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中 DevCon 显示 DiskDrive 类的上一级筛选器驱动程序并且确认它没有更改它们。在本例中，此显示显示 DiskDrive 安装程序类中使用 PartMgr.sys 上一级筛选器驱动程序的设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-55" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_9a1ac77b-288b-4e35-9c0b-7bf5abb93d85" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">Class filters unchanged.
    PartMgr

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_24_add_a_filter_driver_to_a_setup_class_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_24_ADD_A_FILTER_DRIVER_TO_A_SETUP_CLASS_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 24：向某个安装程序类中添加筛选器驱动程序
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544714" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon ClassFilter
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作向 DiskDrive 安装程序类中的上一级筛选器驱动程序列表中添加一个虚构的筛选器 Disklog.sys。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      该命令使用 add-after (
      <strong>
       +
      </strong>
      ) ClassFilter 运算符加载 PartMgr 驱动程序之后的 Disklog 驱动程序，以便它收到 PartMgr.sys 已处理的数据。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      启动该命令之后，将虚拟光标放置在第一个筛选器驱动程序前面。由于没有放置在特定驱动程序上，因此 DevCon 将 Disklog 驱动程序添加到筛选器驱动程序列表的结尾。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      该命令还使用
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数，该参数会在必要时重新启动系统以使类筛选器更改生效。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-56" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_2a224580-5b82-4709-bb4f-b8c337dd0484" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /r classfilter DiskDrive upper +Disklog

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 DiskDrive 类的当前上一级筛选器驱动程序。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-57" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_0390a123-bff0-4f18-a6cb-1ec9d0bef456" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">Class filters changed. Class devices must be restarted for changes to take effect.
    PartMgr
    Disklog

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      如果驱动程序名称的拼写错误，或者尝试添加系统上未安装的驱动程序，那么该命令会失败。DevCon 不会添加驱动程序，除非该驱动程序注册为服务，也就是说，除非该驱动程序在 Services 注册表子项 (HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\System\CurrentControlSet\Services) 中有一个子项。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令测试此保护功能。该命令尝试将“Disklgg”（而不是“Disklog”）添加到 DiskDrive 类的上一级筛选器列表中。输出表明该命令失败了。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-58" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_faff7010-a49d-49d0-960e-6ba9a3b7b8af" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /r classfilter DiskDrive upper +Disklgg
devcon failed.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_25_insert_a_filter_driver_in_the_class_list_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_25_INSERT_A_FILTER_DRIVER_IN_THE_CLASS_LIST_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 25：在类列表中插入筛选器驱动程序
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544714" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon ClassFilter
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作向 DiskDrive 安装程序类中的上一级筛选器驱动程序列表中添加一个虚构的筛选器驱动程序 MyFilter.sys。该命令按照加载顺序将 MyFilter.sys 放置在 PartMgr.sys 和 Disklog.sys 中间。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-59" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_838234c9-bf61-4964-9b57-588d3999649f" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /r classfilter DiskDrive upper @Disklog -MyFilter

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下列表显示了提交该命令之前 DiskDrive 类的筛选器驱动程序。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-60" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_a2f16d9f-2963-44d7-965c-26c151ce1ee2" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">    PartMgr
    Disklog

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      第一个子命令
      <strong>
       @Disklog
      </strong>
      使用定位运算符 (
      <strong>
       @
      </strong>
      ) 将虚拟光标放置在 Disklog 筛选器驱动程序上。第二个子命令
      <strong>
       -MyFilter
      </strong>
      使用 add-before 运算符 (
      <strong>
       -
      </strong>
      ) 将 MyFilter.sys 添加到 Disklog.sys 前面。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      该命令还使用
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数，该参数会在必要时重新启动系统以使类筛选器更改生效。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      定位运算符在本例中是必不可少的。在 DevCon 处理任何 classfilter 子命令之前，虚拟光标位于列表的开头处，因此未放置在任何筛选器驱动程序上。当光标未在某个驱动程序上时，如果使用 add-before (
      <strong>
       +
      </strong>
      ) 运算符，DevCon 会将该驱动程序添加到列表的开头处。当光标未在某个驱动程序上时，如果使用 add-after (
      <strong>
       -
      </strong>
      ) 运算符，DevCon 会将该驱动程序添加到列表的结尾处。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 DiskDrive 类的当前上一级筛选器驱动程序。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-61" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_553d7cbc-22a6-4b31-b5d5-3b208614a3dc" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">Class filters changed. Class devices must be restarted for changes to take effect.
    PartMgr
    MyFilter
    Disklog

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      也可以使用以下命令添加 MyFilter 驱动程序并将该驱动程序放置在 PartMgr 和 Disklog 之间。在本例中，第一个子命令
      <strong>
       @PartMgr
      </strong>
      将虚拟光标放置在 PartMgr 筛选器驱动程序上。第二个子命令
      <strong>
       +MyFilter
      </strong>
      使用 add-after 运算符 (+) 将 MyFilter.sys 添加到 PartMgr 后面。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-62" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_d4d6822c-e1ce-4e1f-8ffa-24766f79db7e" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /r classfilter DiskDrive upper @PartMgr +MyFilter

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_26_replace_a_filter_driver_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_26_REPLACE_A_FILTER_DRIVER_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 26：替换筛选器驱动程序
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544714" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon ClassFilter
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作将 DiskDrive 安装程序类的筛选器驱动程序列表中 MyFilter.sys 的原始副本替换为新的、改进的版本 MyNewFilter.sys。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-63" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_84ad1d4d-2455-46a6-8c78-b0e718e21fbc" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /r classfilter DiskDrive upper !MyFilter +MyNewFilter

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下列表显示了提交该命令之前 DiskDrive 类的筛选器驱动程序。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-64" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_a46860a7-fa88-40a2-bcd8-f4d2fdf6a356" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">    PartMgr
    MyFilter
    Disklog

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      第一个子命令使用删除运算符 (
      <strong>
       !
      </strong>
      ) 将 MyFilter 从 DiskDrive 类的上一级筛选器驱动程序列表中删除。（它不会影响 C:\Windows\System32\Drivers 目录中的 MyFilter.sys 文件。）
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      第二个子命令使用 add-after 运算符 (
      <strong>
       +
      </strong>
      ) 将新的筛选器驱动程序放置在已删除的驱动程序所在的位置。由于删除运算符将光标放置在已删除筛选器所在的位置，因此 add-before (
      <strong>
       -
      </strong>
      ) 和 add-after (
      <strong>
       +
      </strong>
      ) 运算符具有相同的效果。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      该命令还使用
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数，该参数会在必要时重新启动系统以使类筛选器更改生效。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 DiskDrive 类的新的类筛选器配置。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-65" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_d846efb6-2e4f-4c07-8431-cbed3b9d03bb" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">Class filters changed. Class devices must be restarted for changes to take effect.
    PartMgr
    MyNewFilter
    Disklog

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_27_change_the_order_of_filter_drivers_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_27_CHANGE_THE_ORDER_OF_FILTER_DRIVERS_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 27：更改筛选器驱动程序的顺序
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544714" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon ClassFilter
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作更改 DiskDrive 安装程序类的筛选器驱动程序的顺序。具体来说，它颠倒了第二个和第三个筛选器驱动程序的顺序。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-66" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_43c66f4f-1fb0-464d-80a8-d9566fbd817d" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /r classfilter DiskDrive upper !Disklog =@PartMgr +Disklog

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下列表显示了提交该命令之前 DiskDrive 类的筛选器驱动程序。它还显示了该命令的预期结果。
     </p>
     <table style="border-collapse:collapse; margin-bottom:20px; margin-top:20px; padding:0px; width:938px; border:1px solid rgb(187,187,187)">
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <th style="padding:10px 8px; color:rgb(99,99,99); border:1px solid rgb(187,187,187); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important; background-color:rgb(237,237,237)">
         之前
        </th>
        <th style="padding:10px 8px; color:rgb(99,99,99); border:1px solid rgb(187,187,187); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important; background-color:rgb(237,237,237)">
         之后
        </th>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important; padding:10px 8px; color:rgb(42,42,42); vertical-align:top; border:1px solid rgb(187,187,187)">
         <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:0px; line-height:18px">
          PartMgr
         </p>
        </td>
        <td style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important; padding:10px 8px; color:rgb(42,42,42); vertical-align:top; border:1px solid rgb(187,187,187)">
         <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:0px; line-height:18px">
          PartMgr
         </p>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important; padding:10px 8px; color:rgb(42,42,42); vertical-align:top; border:1px solid rgb(187,187,187)">
         <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:0px; line-height:18px">
          MyNewFilter
         </p>
        </td>
        <td style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important; padding:10px 8px; color:rgb(42,42,42); vertical-align:top; border:1px solid rgb(187,187,187)">
         <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:0px; line-height:18px">
          Disklog
         </p>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important; padding:10px 8px; color:rgb(42,42,42); vertical-align:top; border:1px solid rgb(187,187,187)">
         <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:0px; line-height:18px">
          Disklog
         </p>
        </td>
        <td style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important; padding:10px 8px; color:rgb(42,42,42); vertical-align:top; border:1px solid rgb(187,187,187)">
         <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:0px; line-height:18px">
          MyNewFilter
         </p>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      第一个子命令使用删除运算符 (
      <strong>
       !)
      </strong>
      ) 从列表中删除 Disklog。第二个子命令使用启动运算符 (
      <strong>
       =)
      </strong>
      ) 将虚拟光标移回起始位置，然后使用定位运算符 (
      <strong>
       @)
      </strong>
      ) 将光标放置在 PartMgr 驱动程序上。启动运算符是必需的，因为虚拟光标仅在列表中向前移动。最后一个子命令使用 add-after 运算符 (
      <strong>
       +)
      </strong>
      ) 将 Disklog 添加到 PartMgr 后面。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 DiskDrive 类的新的类筛选器配置。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-67" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_7460ba7e-e49a-4dc8-a131-d06bee07efd1" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">Class filters changed. Class devices must be restarted for changes to take effect.
    PartMgr
    Disklog
    MyNewFilter

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_28_enable_a_particular_device_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_28_ENABLE_A_PARTICULAR_DEVICE_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 28：启用特定设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544741" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Enable
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作启用已禁止纠正系统问题的可编程中断控制器。由于控制器硬件 ID *PNP0000 包含一个星号，因此该命令使用单引号字符 (
      <strong>
       '
      </strong>
      ) 定向 DevCon 以查找与该命令中指定的完全相同的硬件 ID。否则，会将该星号解释为通配符。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-68" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_c4fecf61-ec42-448a-965f-fe9c47b6adcc" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon enable '*PNP0000

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示设备的设备实例 ID 并且注明你必须重新系统才能启用该设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-69" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_8d11373d-33ac-466f-8b4c-b0bab8603b51" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ACPI\PNP0000\4&amp;B4063F4&amp;0                                    : Enabled on reboot
Not all of 1 device(s) enabled, at least one requires reboot to complete the operation.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      你可以手动或使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544791" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Reboot
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作重新启动系统，从而进行响应。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令向上一个命令中添加
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数。仅当完成某个操作需要重新启动时，
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数才会重新启动系统。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-70" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_d0ef947f-c355-4548-8cf0-8d10a33bd65a" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /r enable '*PNP0000

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 启用设备，然后重新启动系统以使启用生效。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      启动系统时，使用 DevCon 状态命令来确认该设备已启用。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-71" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_4d2cea6e-cd71-4fbd-b7a5-c6e199b1b0e0" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon status '*PNP0000

ACPI\PNP0000\4&amp;B4063F4&amp;0
    Name: Programmable interrupt controller
    Driver is running.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_29_enable_devices_by_class_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_29_ENABLE_DEVICES_BY_CLASS_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 29：通过类启用设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令通过在
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544741" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Enable
       </strong>
      </a>
      命令中指定“打印机”安装程序类启用计算机上的所有打印机设备。该命令包含
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数，该参数会在必要时重新启动系统以使启用生效。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-72" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_adc68265-505d-4080-935f-2e6937caa30d" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /r enable =Printer

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示在“打印机”类中找到的打印机的设备实例 ID 并报告该打印机已启用。尽管该命令包含
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数，但是系统并不会重新启动，因为启用打印机不需要重新启动。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-73" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_562d7788-2b29-498d-afea-aecd76ad266b" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">LPTENUM\HEWLETT-PACKARDDESKJET_1120C\1&amp;7530F08&amp;0&amp;LPT1.4        : Enabled
1 device(s) enabled.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_30_disable_devices_by_an_id_pattern_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_30_DISABLE_DEVICES_BY_AN_ID_PATTERN_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 30：通过 ID 模式禁用设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544722" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Disable
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作禁用本地计算机上的 USB 设备。该命令通过硬件 ID 模式 (USB*) 来标识设备。该模式将与其硬件 ID 或兼容的 ID 以“USB”开头的任何设备匹配。该命令包含
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数，该参数会在必要时重新启动系统以使禁用生效。
     </p>
     <div class="note">
      <strong>
       注意
      </strong>
      使用 ID 模式禁用设备之前，确定哪些设备将受到影响。为此，在显示命令中使用该模式，如
      <strong>
       devcon status USB*
      </strong>
      或
      <strong>
       devcon hwids USB*
      </strong>
      。
     </div>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-74" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_8677ba3b-c986-45ce-8457-600320239cd6" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /r disable USB*

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 USB 设备的设备实例 ID 并报告这些设备已禁用。尽管该命令包含
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数，但是系统并不会重新启动，因为禁用这些设备不需要重新启动。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-75" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_9b686b99-4147-4386-a049-f83c7ec2af19" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">USB\ROOT_HUB\4&amp;2A40B465&amp;0
: Disabled
USB\ROOT_HUB\4&amp;7EFA360&amp;0
: Disabled
USB\VID_045E&amp;PID_0039\5&amp;29F428A4&amp;0&amp;2
: Disabled
3 device(s) disabled.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_31_disable_devices_by_device_instance_id_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_31_DISABLE_DEVICES_BY_DEVICE_INSTANCE_ID_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 31：通过设备实例 ID 禁用设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544722" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Disable
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作禁用本地计算机上的 USB 设备。该命令通过其设备实例 ID 来标识设备，这些 ID 由每个 ID 前面的 at 字符 (
      <strong>
       @
      </strong>
      ) 所指示。每个设备实例 ID 与其他设备实例 ID 之间用一个空格分隔。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      而且，由于设备实例 ID 包含 &amp; 字符 (
      <strong>
       &amp;
      </strong>
      )，因此它们应包含在引号中。该命令包含
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数，该参数会在必要时重新启动系统以使禁用生效。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-76" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_73c80b05-a608-4aa7-8652-5d5f5859bb30" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /r disable "@USB\ROOT_HUB\4&amp;2A40B465&amp;0" "@USB\ROOT_HUB\4&amp;7EFA360&amp;0" "@USB\VID_045E&amp;PID_0039\5&amp;29F428A4&amp;0&amp;2"

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 USB 设备的设备实例 ID 并报告这些设备已禁用。尽管该命令包含
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数，但是系统并不会重新启动，因为禁用这些设备不需要重新启动。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-77" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_0f3e14fb-b955-4c2d-a81a-c04a8abe3eeb" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">USB\ROOT_HUB\4&amp;2A40B465&amp;0
: Disabled
USB\ROOT_HUB\4&amp;7EFA360&amp;0
: Disabled
USB\VID_045E&amp;PID_0039\5&amp;29F428A4&amp;0&amp;2
: Disabled
3 device(s) disabled.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_32_update_the_driver_for_communication_ports_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_32_UPDATE_THE_DRIVER_FOR_COMMUNICATION_PORTS_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 32：更新通信端口的驱动程序
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544832" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Update
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作将系统上通信端口的当前设备驱动程序替换为 test.inf 文件中指定的测试驱动程序。该命令只影响其整个硬件 ID 为 *PNP0501（包括星号）的设备。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      你可以使用该命令将系统上签名的驱动程序替换为备用驱动程序以便进行测试或疑难解答，或者将设备与最新版本的相同驱动程序相关联。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-78" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_8359b19f-5fd9-4fcc-ae07-36ec097cd8f7" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon update c:\windows\inf\test.inf *PNP0501

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示一个“硬件安装”
      <strong>
      </strong>
      警告，该警告表明该驱动程序未通过 Windows 徽标测试。如果单击该对话框上的“仍要继续”
      <strong>
      </strong>
      按钮，会继续安装。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      然后，DevCon 显示以下成功消息。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-79" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_3455bc07-8093-4a93-bdb3-d43af40ed388" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">Updating drivers for *PNP0501 from c:\windows\inf\test.inf.
Drivers updated successfully.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      也可以使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544835" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon UpdateNI
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作（即
      <strong>
       DevCon Update
      </strong>
      操作的非交互版本）来更新驱动程序。
      <strong>
       DevCon UpdateNI
      </strong>
      操作等同于
      <strong>
       DevCon Update
      </strong>
      操作，但它会抑制需要响应的所有用户提示，并且假定提示的默认响应。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <strong>
       DevCon UpdateNI
      </strong>
      操作安装测试驱动程序。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-80" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_752c6954-45a0-4556-868a-bb29d99bfd41" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon updateni c:\windows\inf\test.inf *PNP0501

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在本例中，DevCon 不显示“硬件安装”
      <strong>
      </strong>
      警告。而是假定默认的响应“停止安装”
      <strong>
      </strong>
      。因此，DevCon 无法更新驱动程序并且显示一个失败消息。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-81" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_52e71721-06cc-495e-9665-da9e70a997f2" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">Updating drivers for *PNP0501 from c:\windows\inf\test.inf.
devcon failed.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_33_install_a_device_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_33_INSTALL_A_DEVICE_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 33：安装设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544780" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Install
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作在本地计算机上安装键盘设备。该命令包含到该设备的 INF 文件的完整路径 (keyboard.inf) 和一个硬件 ID (*PNP030b)。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-82" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_02661cfb-bd9e-48a8-8369-51472f067ef4" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /r install c:\windows\inf\keyboard.inf *PNP030b

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 报告它已安装该设备，也就是说，它已为新的设备创建了设备节点并且为该设备创建了更新的驱动程序文件。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-83" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
