      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_a6799b2f-2ce7-48ee-a56e-70dd8b7365ac" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">Device node created. Install is complete when drivers files are updated...
Updating drivers for *PNPO30b from c:\windows\inf\keyboard.inf
Drivers updated successfully.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_34_install_a_device_using_unattended_setup_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_34_INSTALL_A_DEVICE_USING_UNATTENDED_SETUP_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 34：使用无人参与安装来安装设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下示例显示在无人参与安装 Microsoft Windows XP 期间如何安装 Microsoft 环回适配器。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      若要在无人参与安装期间安装此设备，请首先向软盘中添加以下文件：devcon.exe 和 netloop.inf (C:\Windows\inf\netloop.inf)。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      然后，向无人参与安装文件的
      <strong>
       [GUIRunOnce]
      </strong>
      部分中添加以下 DevCon 命令：
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-84" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_a2a640a0-1215-4347-bae4-e0c71a253f08" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">a:\devcon /r install a:\Netloop.inf '*MSLOOP

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      该命令使用其硬件 ID *MSLOOP 来标识环回适配器。“*MSLOOP”前面的单引号字符告知 DevCon 按照字义解释该字符串，也就是说将星号解释为硬件 ID 的一部分，而不是解释为通配符。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      该命令还指定 DevCon 在安装中使用 Netloop.inf 文件（位于软盘上）。仅当必须重新启动才能完成安装时，
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数才会重新启动计算机。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      最后，向无人参与安装文件中添加网络配置设置并运行无人参与安装。
     </p>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_35_remove_devices_by_device_instance_id_pattern_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_35_REMOVE_DEVICES_BY_DEVICE_INSTANCE_ID_PATTERN_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 35：通过设备实例 ID 模式删除设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544796" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Remove
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作删除计算机中的所有 USB 设备。该命令通过设备实例 ID 模式来标识设备，该模式与以“USB\”字符串开头的任何设备实例 ID（注册表路径）都匹配。at 字符 (
      <strong>
       @
      </strong>
      ) 将设备实例 ID 与硬件 ID 或兼容的 ID 区分开来。该命令也包含
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数，该参数会在需要时重新启动系统以使删除过程生效。
     </p>
     <div class="note">
      <strong>
       警告
      </strong>
      使用某个模式删除任何设备之前，确定哪些设备会受到影响。为此，在显示命令中使用该模式，如
      <strong>
       devcon status @usb\*
      </strong>
      或
      <strong>
       devcon hwids @usb\*
      </strong>
      。
     </div>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-85" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_6742a19e-c903-4911-b150-530054700c55" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /r remove @usb\*

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示已删除的设备的设备实例 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-86" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_18966d01-e8f9-4eb9-9efa-7879d38d0b05" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">USB\ROOT_HUB\4&amp;2A40B465&amp;0                             : Removed
USB\ROOT_HUB\4&amp;7EFA360&amp;0                              : Removed
USB\VID_045E&amp;PID_0039\5&amp;29F428A4&amp;0&amp;2                  : Removed
3 device(s) removed.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_36_remove_a_particular_network_device_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_36_REMOVE_A_PARTICULAR_NETWORK_DEVICE_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 36：删除特定的网络设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544796" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Remove
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作从本地计算机上卸载 NDISWAN 微型端口驱动程序。该命令指定 Net 类，然后通过指定该类中的设备（其硬件 ID 或兼容的 ID 包含“ndiswan”）来改进搜索。该命令也包含
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数，该参数会在需要时重新启动系统以使删除过程生效。
     </p>
     <div class="note">
      <strong>
       警告
      </strong>
      使用某个模式删除任何设备之前，确定哪些设备会受到影响。为此，在显示命令中使用该模式，如
      <strong>
       devcon status =net *ndiswan*
      </strong>
      或
      <strong>
       devcon hwids =net *ndiswan*
      </strong>
      。
     </div>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-87" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_65821630-849e-42c5-ba24-3d2da30f1443" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /r remove =net *ndiswan*

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示已删除的设备的设备实例 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-88" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_f0d4836c-1df7-4aa0-86ca-4d2db7b09cf4" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ROOT\MS_NDISWANIP\0000 : Removed 1 device(s) removed.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_37_scan_the_computer_for_new_devices_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_37_SCAN_THE_COMPUTER_FOR_NEW_DEVICES_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 37：扫描计算机中的新设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544799" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Rescan
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作扫描本地计算机中的新设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-89" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_2c98952f-d4a2-4d66-a5d5-d23775c0b19e" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon rescan

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 报告它已扫描系统，但未发现任何新设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-90" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_3a2155cd-f15b-47b6-abf0-1f53082bcd5e" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">Scanning for new hardware.
Scanning completed.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      也可以在远程计算机上使用
      <strong>
       DevCon Rescan
      </strong>
      命令。以下命令通过向命令中添加
      <strong>
       /m
      </strong>
      参数在远程计算机 Server01 上运行
      <strong>
       DevCon Rescan
      </strong>
      操作。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-91" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_78dca26e-60cd-4cf4-a67b-17862e4aedb7" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /m:\\server01 rescan

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_38_restart_a_device_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_38_RESTART_A_DEVICE_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 38：重新启动设备
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544807" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Restart
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作在本地计算机上重新启动环回适配器。该命令将搜索限制于 Net 安装程序类，并且在该类中，指定环回适配器的设备实例 ID
      <strong>
       ROOT\*MSLOOP\0000
      </strong>
      。at 字符 (
      <strong>
       @
      </strong>
      ) 将此字符串标识为设备实例 ID。请求字义搜索的单引号字符 (
      <strong>
       '
      </strong>
      ), 防止 DevCon 将 ID 中的星号解释为通配符字符。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-92" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_c270a477-c613-4a75-a20d-ec1184a8a75b" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon restart =net @'ROOT\*MSLOOP\0000

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示设备的设备实例 ID 并报告结果。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-93" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_ba04c403-a551-4cab-bb83-7f54c6a3b91b" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ROOT\*MSLOOP\0000                                              : Restarted
1 device(s) restarted.

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_39_reboot_the_local_computer_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_39_REBOOT_THE_LOCAL_COMPUTER_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 39：重新启动本地计算机
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544791" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Reboot
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作在本地计算机上重新启动操作系统并将重新启动与硬件安装相关联。与
      <strong>
       /r
      </strong>
      参数不同，
      <strong>
       DevCon Reboot
      </strong>
      操作不依赖于另一个操作的返回代码。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      可以将该命令包含在需要重新启动系统的脚本和批处理文件中。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-94" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_55739456-cdeb-4d5c-b64e-e74b1749be7c" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon reboot

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示一条表明正在重新启动计算机的消息（正在重新启动本地计算机）。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-95" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_5653195e-ba2a-4521-9ec6-b890c0b17884" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important"></pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      DevCon 使用标准的
      <strong>
       ExitWindowsEx
      </strong>
      函数来重新启动。如果用户已在计算机上打开文件或者某个程序未关闭，那么系统不会重新启动，直到用户对关闭这些文件或结束该进程的系统提示进行响应为止。
     </p>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_40_assign_a_hardware_id_to_a_legacy_device_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_40_ASSIGN_A_HARDWARE_ID_TO_A_LEGACY_DEVICE_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 40：为旧设备分配硬件 ID
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544825" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon SetHwID
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作将硬件 ID beep 分配给旧的蜂鸣设备。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      该命令使用设备的设备实例 ID ROOT\LEGACY_BEEP\0000，因为旧的蜂鸣设备没有硬件 ID 或兼容的 ID。该命令使用 at 字符 (
      <strong>
       @
      </strong>
      ) 指示该字符串为设备实例 ID。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      该命令不会使用任何符号参数来定位 ID。默认情况下，DevCon 将新的硬件 ID 添加到硬件 ID 列表的结尾处。在本例中，由于设备没有其他硬件 ID，因此与位置无关。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-96" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_8fd97779-3ad5-4ff5-b709-83cd44734230" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon sethwid @ROOT\LEGACY_BEEP\0000 := beep

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示一条消息，该消息指出已向设备的硬件 ID 列表中添加了 beep。还显示所得到的硬件 ID 列表。在本例中，列表中只有一个硬件 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-97" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_2a84069b-a6a6-4c58-9363-2f4d1e612cd9" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ROOT\LEGACY_BEEP\0000                              : beep
Modified 1 hardware ID(s).

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_41_add_a_hardware_id_to_all_legacy_devices_on_a_remote_com" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_41_ADD_A_HARDWARE_ID_TO_ALL_LEGACY_DEVICES_ON_A_REMOTE_COM" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 41：为远程计算机上的所有旧设备添加硬件 ID
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544825" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon SetHwID
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作将硬件 ID legacy 添加到远程计算机 Server1 上所有旧设备的硬件 ID 列表中。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      该命令使用
      <strong>
       -
      </strong>
      符号参数将新的硬件 ID 添加到设备的硬件 ID 列表的结尾处（如果已为其中一个设备创建了首选的硬件 ID）。该命令使用
      <strong>
       /m
      </strong>
      参数来指定远程计算机。它还使用设备实例 ID 模式
      <strong>
       @ROOT\LEGACY*
      </strong>
      标识计算机上的旧设备，即，其设备实例 ID 以
      <strong>
       ROOT\LEGACY
      </strong>
      开头的所有设备。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-98" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_fa84688b-b405-415e-875b-52fcaf38e520" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /m:\\Server1 sethwid @ROOT\LEGACY* := -legacy

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示所有受影响的设备的结果硬件 ID 列表。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-99" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_5824cf7f-1e11-4967-bfda-3420b73db8ec" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ROOT\LEGACY_AFD\0000                                        : legacy
ROOT\LEGACY_BEEP\0000                                    : beep,legacy
ROOT\LEGACY_CRCDISK\0000                                    : legacy
ROOT\LEGACY_DMBOOT\0000                                     : legacy
ROOT\LEGACY_DMLOAD\0000                                     : legacy
ROOT\LEGACY_FIPS\0000                                       : legacy
...
ROOT\LEGACY_WANARP\0000                                     : legacy
Modified 27 hardware ID(s).

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      为一组设备分配相同的硬件 ID 之后，你可以使用其他 DevCon 操作在一个命令中查看和更改设备。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      例如，以下命令显示了所有旧设备的状态。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-100" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_bd068637-b914-4db9-916f-9aad59338ee1" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon status legacy

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_42_delete_a_hardware_id_from_all_legacy_devices_on_a_remot" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_42_DELETE_A_HARDWARE_ID_FROM_ALL_LEGACY_DEVICES_ON_A_REMOT" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 42：从远程计算机上的所有旧设备中删除硬件 ID
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544825" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon SetHwID
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作将硬件 ID
      <strong>
       legacy
      </strong>
      从远程计算机 Server1 上所有旧设备的硬件 ID 列表中删除。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      此命令使用
      <strong>
       /m
      </strong>
      参数来指定远程计算机。它使用硬件 ID
      <strong>
       legacy
      </strong>
      来标识具有该硬件 ID 的所有设备。然后，它使用
      <strong>
       !
      </strong>
      符号参数删除
      <strong>
       legacy
      </strong>
      硬件 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-101" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_5d3d46e8-90d7-4d58-8202-b53b9b8fc16f" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon /m:\\Server1 sethwid legacy := !legacy

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示所有受影响的设备的结果硬件 ID 列表。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-102" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_d479c508-26ab-40cd-8cfa-63d6cfae9d39" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ROOT\LEGACY_AFD\0000                                        :
ROOT\LEGACY_BEEP\0000                                    : beep
ROOT\LEGACY_CRCDISK\0000                                    :
ROOT\LEGACY_DMBOOT\0000                                     :
ROOT\LEGACY_DMLOAD\0000                                     :
ROOT\LEGACY_FIPS\0000                                       :
...
ROOT\LEGACY_WANARP\0000                                     :
Modified 27 hardware ID(s).

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_43_add_delete_and_replace_hardwareids_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_43_ADD_DELETE_AND_REPLACE_HARDWAREIDS_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 43：添加、删除和替换硬件 ID
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      下面的一系列示例显示了如何使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544825" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon SetHwID
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作的各种功能。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      此系列使用一个虚构的设备 DeviceX，其设备实例 ID 为
      <strong>
       ROOT\DeviceX\0000
      </strong>
      。使用 DevCon 之前，该设备具有以下硬件 ID 列表：
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-103" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_239ffe29-9f53-41a2-8668-74e6058ac6dc" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">Hw3 Hw4

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <strong>
       +
      </strong>
      符号将
      <strong>
       Hw1
      </strong>
      和
      <strong>
       Hw2
      </strong>
      添加到 DeviceX 的硬件 ID 列表的开头处。由于
      <strong>
       Hw2
      </strong>
      已出现在列表中，因此只是进行移动，而不是添加。该命令通过其设备实例 ID 来标识设备，这些 ID 由每个 ID 前面的 at 字符 (
      <strong>
       @
      </strong>
      ) 所指示。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-104" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_93218ed7-28b6-458d-b3f6-245120dea72e" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon sethwid @ROOT\DEVICEX\0000 := +Hw1 Hw2

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示设备的新硬件 ID 列表。请注意，
      <strong>
       Hw1
      </strong>
      和
      <strong>
       Hw2
      </strong>
      按照指定的顺序出现在列表的开头处。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-105" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_0c3a4911-0424-4a97-b13c-3040e548df28" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ROOT\DEVICEX\0000                         : Hw1,Hw2,Hw3,Hw4
Modified 1 hardware ID(s).

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      而且，DevCon 报告它已修改一个硬件 ID 列表，即，一个设备的硬件 ID 列表。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <strong>
       !
      </strong>
      符号删除
      <strong>
       Hw1
      </strong>
      硬件 ID。然后，它不使用任何符号参数列出硬件 ID
      <strong>
       Hw5
      </strong>
      。如果不使用符号参数，SetHwID 会将硬件 ID 添加到设备的硬件 ID 列表的结尾处。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      该命令演示了这种情况，与
      <strong>
       DevCon SetHwID
      </strong>
      操作的其他符号参数不同，
      <strong>
       !
      </strong>
      参数仅应用于使用它作为前缀的硬件 ID.
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-106" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_04a5daef-527f-4fa6-ae82-64d6f88dd1ab" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon sethwid @ROOT\DeviceX\0000 := !Hw1 Hw5

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 DeviceX 的结果硬件 ID 列表。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-107" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_c05f8f8f-74d1-42ab-9502-6dc80d6596bf" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ROOT\DEVICEX\0000                         : Hw2,Hw3,Hw4,Hw5
Modified 1 hardware ID(s).

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用 = 参数将 DeviceX 的所有硬件 ID 列表替换为一个硬件 ID
      <strong>
       DevX
      </strong>
      。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-108" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_bf641d55-3e4b-475b-8507-bb4068186ac7" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon sethwid @ROOT\DeviceX\0000 := =DevX

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 DeviceX 的结果硬件 ID 列表。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-109" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_ed4d996d-7706-4206-8f3e-2cdbf29c8414" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ROOT\DEVICEX\0000                         : DevX
Modified 1 hardware ID(s).

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      成功消息指示 DevCon 已修改一个设备的硬件 ID。
     </p>
     <h4 style="font-family:'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:1.386em; font-weight:normal; margin:0px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-top:5px">
      <a id="ddk_example_44_forcibly_update_the_hal_tools" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      <a id="DDK_EXAMPLE_44_FORCIBLY_UPDATE_THE_HAL_TOOLS" style="color:rgb(0,116,158); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI','Lucida Grande',Verdana,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif!important" target="_blank">
      </a>
      示例 44：强制更新 HAL
     </h4>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下示例显示如何使用 DevCon 更新计算机上的 HAL。在该示例中，测试人员希望将该计算机最适合的单处理器 APCI APIC HAL 替换为多处理器 APCI APIC HAL 以便进行测试。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      第一个命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544825" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon SetHwID
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作将 HAL 的硬件 ID 从
      <strong>
       acpiapic_up
      </strong>
      （单处理器 HAL 的硬件 ID）更改为
      <strong>
       acpiapic_mp
      </strong>
      （多处理器 HAL 的硬件 ID）。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      必须更改硬件 ID，因为 HAL 的 INF 文件包含单处理器和多处理器 HAL 的驱动程序。系统根据设备的硬件 ID 从 INF 文件中选择最合适的驱动程序。如果不更改硬件 ID，那么
      <strong>
       DevCon Update
      </strong>
      命令将只是重新安装单处理器 HAL 驱动程序。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在以下命令中，该命令通过它的实例 ID
      <strong>
       ROOT\ACPI_HAL\0000
      </strong>
      来标识 HAL，该 ID 由 ID 前面的
      <strong>
       @
      </strong>
      字符所指示。该命令使用
      <strong>
       +
      </strong>
      字符使
      <strong>
       acpiapic_mp
      </strong>
      成为 HAL 硬件 ID 列表中的第一个硬件 ID。然后，它使用
      <strong>
       !
      </strong>
      字符从 HAL 的硬件 ID 列表中删除
      <strong>
       acpiapic_up
      </strong>
      硬件 ID。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-110" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_45641e5b-d60f-4359-8592-501f9a8ee9b0" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon sethwid @ROOT\ACPI_HAL\0000 := +acpiapic_mp !acpiapic_up

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      在响应中，DevCon 显示 HAL 的以下新硬件 ID 列表。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-111" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_22730858-5e60-4ebe-9c9b-47e51b86244c" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">ROOT\ACPI_HAL\0000                         : acpiapic_mp
Modified 1 hardware ID(s).

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      以下命令使用
      <a href="https://technet.microsoft.com/zh-cn/library/ff544832" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="text-decoration:none; color:rgb(0,102,221)" target="_blank">
       <strong>
        DevCon Update
       </strong>
      </a>
      操作更新 HAL 的驱动程序。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-112" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_21dbc16c-04ea-42fc-83f2-603656e3e142" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">devcon update c:\windows\inf\hal.inf acpiapic_mp

</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-bottom:15px; line-height:18px">
      然后，DevCon 显示以下成功消息。
     </p>
     <div class="codeSnippetContainer" id="code-snippet-113" style="min-width:260px; clear:both">
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerTabs" style="vertical-align:middle; height:23px; position:relative; z-index:1">
      </div>
      <div class="codeSnippetContainerCodeContainer" style="border:1px solid rgb(147,147,147); clear:both; margin-bottom:12px; position:relative; top:-1px">
       <div class="codeSnippetToolBar" style="width:auto; height:auto">
        <div class="codeSnippetToolBarText" style="float:right; top:-8px; position:relative; width:auto; padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px; height:0px; vertical-align:top">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="codeSnippetContainerCode" dir="ltr" id="CodeSnippetContainerCode_32c1f521-6409-4e69-b015-33b9fe5a9147" style="width:auto; margin:0px; padding:10px 21px">
        <div style="padding:0px; margin:0px; color:black">
         <pre style="padding:5px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; overflow:auto; word-wrap:normal; font-family:Consolas,Courier,monospace!important">Updating drivers for acpiapic_mp from c:\windows\inf\hal.inf.
Drivers updated successfully.</pre>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>
   </div>
  </div>
